Run # Find any available iOS Simulator device
  # Find any available iOS Simulator device
  DEVICE_ID=$(xcrun simctl list devices available 2>/dev/null | \
    grep -E 'iPad|iPhone' | grep -v 'unavailable' | \
    grep -oE '[0-9A-F-]{36}' | head -1)
  if [ -z "$DEVICE_ID" ]; then
    echo "No iOS Simulator available — skipping build check"
    exit 0
  fi
  echo "Building for simulator: $(xcrun simctl list devices available 2>/dev/null | grep "$DEVICE_ID")"
  xcodebuild build \
    -scheme Inscribe \
    -destination "platform=iOS Simulator,id=$DEVICE_ID" \
    -configuration Debug \
    CODE_SIGNING_ALLOWED=NO 2>&1 | tee xcodebuild_sim_check.log
  shell: /bin/bash -e {0}
